    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom ddgs import DDGS\nimport time\n\nprint("=== FRENCH TV ARCHIVES SEARCH: FINAL INVESTIGATION ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Find French TV films (1960s-1990s) with children\'s perspectives, goldfish symbolism, societal critique")\nprint("Focus: INA, BNF archives and avant-garde directors (Blin, Serreau, Régy, Chabert)\\n")\n\n# First, inspect existing investigation files to understand current findings\nprint("=== INSPECTING EXISTING INVESTIGATION FILES ===\\n")\n\nfinal_investigation_file = os.path.join(\'workspace\', \'french_tv_film_final_investigation.json\')\nif os.path.exists(final_investigation_file):\n    print(f"Found: {final_investigation_file}")\n    try:\n        with open(final_investigation_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            investigation_data = json.load(f)\n        \n        print("File structure:")\n        for key in investigation_data.keys():\n            print(f"  - {key}")\n        \n        # Extract key information about top candidate\n        if \'top_candidate\' in investigation_data:\n            top_candidate = investigation_data[\'top_candidate\']\n            if \'candidate\' in top_candidate:\n                candidate_info = top_candidate[\'candidate\']\n                print(f"\\nTop candidate from previous investigation:")\n                print(f"  Title: {candidate_info.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                print(f"  URL: {candidate_info.get(\'url\', \'No URL\')}")\n                print(f"  Description: {candidate_info.get(\'description\', \'No description\')[:200]}...")\n        \n        if \'confidence_assessment\' in investigation_data:\n            confidence = investigation_data[\'confidence_assessment\']\n            print(f"\\nConfidence assessment:")\n            print(f"  Match score: {confidence.get(\'match_score\', \'Unknown\')}")\n            print(f"  Confidence level: {confidence.get(\'confidence_level\', \'Unknown\')}")\n            \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"Error reading investigation file: {e}")\nelse:\n    print("No previous investigation file found")\n\nprint("\\n=== CONDUCTING TARGETED FRENCH ARCHIVE SEARCHES ===\\n")\n\n# Define focused search queries for French TV archives and directors\nsearch_queries = [\n    # Direct searches for the identified candidate\n    \'"Six fois deux" Godard 1976 INA television children goldfish\',\n    \'Jean-Luc Godard "Six fois deux" 1976 enfants poisson rouge\',\n    \n    # INA archive searches\n    \'INA "Institut National Audiovisuel" television film children goldfish 1970s\',\n    \'INA archives French TV film enfants poisson rouge 1960s 1970s 1980s\',\n    \n    # BNF archive searches\n    \'BNF "Bibliothèque nationale" television film children avant-garde France\',\n    \n    # Director-specific searches\n    \'Roger Blin television film children France 1960s 1970s\',\n    \'Jean-Marie Serreau television French film children goldfish\',\n    \'Claude Régy television film children societal critique France\',\n    \n    # Thematic combination searches\n    \'French television film children goldfish symbolism 1960s 1970s 1980s 1990s\',\n    \'télévision française enfants poisson rouge critique sociale avant-garde\'\n]\n\nsearcher = DDGS(timeout=15)\nall_results = []\nrelevant_candidates = []\n\nfor i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):\n    print(f"=== SEARCH {i}/{len(search_queries)} ===")\n    print(f"Query: {query}")\n    \n    try:\n        search_results = searcher.text(\n            query,\n            max_results=8,\n            page=1,\n            backend=["google", "duckduckgo"],\n            safesearch="off",\n            region="fr"\n        )\n        \n        if search_results:\n            print(f"✓ Found {len(search_results)} results")\n            \n            # Analyze each result for relevance\n            for j, result in enumerate(search_results, 1):\n                # Extract result data with defaults\n                result_title = result.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                result_body = result.get(\'body\', \'No body\')\n                result_url = result.get(\'href\', \'No URL\')\n                \n                print(f"\\n  Result {j}:")\n                print(f"    Title: {result_title}")\n                print(f"    URL: {result_url}")\n                print(f"    Body: {result_body[:120]}{\' ...\' if len(result_body) > 120 else \'\'}")\n                \n                # PROPERLY DEFINE analysis_text HERE before using it\n                analysis_text = f"{result_title} {result_body}".lower()\n                \n                # Define keyword categories\n                archive_terms = [\'ina\', \'institut national audiovisuel\', \'bnf\', \'bibliothèque nationale\']\n                tv_terms = [\'télévision\', \'television\', \'tv\', \'film tv\', \'série\']\n                children_terms = [\'enfants\', \'enfant\', \'children\', \'child\', \'kids\', \'louison\']\n                goldfish_terms = [\'poisson rouge\', \'goldfish\', \'poisson\', \'fish\']\n                critique_terms = [\'critique\', \'social\', \'société\', \'societal\', \'avant-garde\']\n                director_terms = [\'roger blin\', \'jean-marie serreau\', \'claude régy\', \'pierre chabert\', \'godard\']\n                era_terms = [\'1960\', \'1970\', \'1980\', \'1990\', \'1976\']\n                \n                # Check for matches using the properly defined analysis_text\n                archive_matches = [term for term in archive_terms if term in analysis_text]\n                tv_matches = [term for term in tv_terms if term in analysis_text]\n                children_matches = [term for term in children_terms if term in analysis_text]\n                goldfish_matches = [term for term in goldfish_terms if term in analysis_text]\n                critique_matches = [term for term in critique_terms if term in analysis_text]\n                director_matches = [term for term in director_terms if term in analysis_text]\n                era_matches = [term for term in era_terms if term in analysis_text]\n                \n                # Calculate relevance score\n                score = 0\n                score += len(archive_matches) * 3  # Archive sources are highly relevant\n                score += len(tv_matches) * 2       # TV medium is essential\n                score += len(children_matches) * 4  # Children themes are key\n                score += len(goldfish_matches) * 4  # Goldfish symbolism is key\n                score += len(critique_matches) * 2  # Societal critique important\n                score += len(director_matches) * 3  # Target directors important\n                score += len(era_matches) * 1       # Era relevance\n                \n                # Display matches found\n                if archive_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** ARCHIVE MATCH: {archive_matches} ***")\n                if tv_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** TV MEDIUM: {tv_matches} ***")\n                if children_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** CHILDREN THEMES: {children_matches} ***")\n                if goldfish_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** GOLDFISH THEMES: {goldfish_matches} ***")\n                if critique_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** CRITIQUE THEMES: {critique_matches} ***")\n                if director_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** DIRECTOR MATCH: {director_matches} ***")\n                if era_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** ERA MATCH: {era_matches} ***")\n                \n                print(f"    Relevance Score: {score}")\n                \n                # Store high-relevance candidates\n                if score >= 6:\n                    print(f"    *** HIGH RELEVANCE CANDIDATE ***")\n                    relevant_candidates.append({\n                        \'title\': result_title,\n                        \'url\': result_url,\n                        \'description\': result_body,\n                        \'relevance_score\': score,\n                        \'archive_matches\': archive_matches,\n                        \'tv_matches\': tv_matches,\n                        \'children_matches\': children_matches,\n                        \'goldfish_matches\': goldfish_matches,\n                        \'critique_matches\': critique_matches,\n                        \'director_matches\': director_matches,\n                        \'era_matches\': era_matches,\n                        \'source_query\': query\n                    })\n            \n            # Store search data\n            search_data = {\n                \'query\': query,\n                \'results_count\': len(search_results),\n                \'results\': search_results\n            }\n            all_results.append(search_data)\n            \n        else:\n            print("✗ No results found")\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"✗ Search failed: {str(e)}")\n    \n    print("-" * 50)\n    time.sleep(1)  # Brief delay between searches\n\nprint(f"\\n=== ANALYSIS OF SEARCH RESULTS ===\\n")\nprint(f"Total searches conducted: {len(search_queries)}")\nprint(f"Total high-relevance candidates found: {len(relevant_candidates)}")\n\nif relevant_candidates:\n    # Sort by relevance score\n    relevant_candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== TOP CANDIDATES ===\\n")\n    \n    for i, candidate in enumerate(relevant_candidates[:3], 1):\n        print(f"Candidate {i} (Score: {candidate[\'relevance_score\']}):")\n        print(f"  Title: {candidate[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"  URL: {candidate[\'url\']}")\n        print(f"  Archive Matches: {candidate[\'archive_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Children Themes: {candidate[\'children_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Goldfish Themes: {candidate[\'goldfish_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Director Matches: {candidate[\'director_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Era Matches: {candidate[\'era_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Description: {candidate[\'description\'][:150]}...")\n        print()\n    \n    # Analyze top candidate\n    top_new_candidate = relevant_candidates[0]\n    \n    print(f"=== TOP CANDIDATE ANALYSIS ===\\n")\n    print(f"Title: {top_new_candidate[\'title\']}")\n    print(f"Relevance Score: {top_new_candidate[\'relevance_score\']}")\n    \n    # Check criteria fulfillment\n    criteria_met = {\n        \'french_tv_production\': len(top_new_candidate[\'archive_matches\']) > 0 or len(top_new_candidate[\'tv_matches\']) > 0,\n        \'target_era_1960s_1990s\': len(top_new_candidate[\'era_matches\']) > 0,\n        \'children_perspectives\': len(top_new_candidate[\'children_matches\']) > 0,\n        \'goldfish_symbolism\': len(top_new_candidate[\'goldfish_matches\']) > 0,\n        \'societal_critique\': len(top_new_candidate[\'critique_matches\']) > 0,\n        \'avant_garde_director\': len(top_new_candidate[\'director_matches\']) > 0\n    }\n    \n    criteria_count = sum(criteria_met.values())\n    print(f"\\nCriteria fulfillment: {criteria_count}/6")\n    \n    for criterion, met in criteria_met.items():\n        status = "✓" if met else "✗"\n        print(f"  {status} {criterion.replace(\'_\', \' \').title()}")\n    \n    # Determine confidence level\n    if criteria_count >= 5:\n        confidence = "Very High"\n    elif criteria_count >= 4:\n        confidence = "High"\n    elif criteria_count >= 3:\n        confidence = "Moderate"\n    else:\n        confidence = "Low"\n    \n    print(f"\\nConfidence Level: {confidence}")\n    \n    # Check if this matches the previously identified candidate\n    if \'godard\' in top_new_candidate[\'title\'].lower() or \'six fois deux\' in top_new_candidate[\'title\'].lower():\n        print(f"\\n*** CONFIRMATION: This matches the previously identified candidate \'Six fois deux\' by Godard ***")\n        \n        # Extract year information\n        year_found = None\n        for era_match in top_new_candidate[\'era_matches\']:\n            if era_match in [\'1976\', \'1970\']:\n                year_found = era_match\n                break\n        \n        if year_found:\n            print(f"*** YEAR CONFIRMED: {year_found} ***")\n        else:\n            print("*** YEAR NEEDS FURTHER VERIFICATION ***")\n\nelse:\n    print("\\nNo high-relevance candidates found in this search.")\n    print("This suggests the film may be:")\n    print("1. The previously identified \'Six fois deux\' by Godard (1976)")\n    print("2. A film not widely indexed in online archives")\n    print("3. Requiring more specialized archive access")\n\n# Save final search results\nfinal_search_results = {\n    \'search_timestamp\': \'2024-12-19\',\n    \'search_objective\': \'Find French TV films (1960s-1990s) with children\\\'s perspectives, goldfish symbolism, and societal critique\',\n    \'methodology\': \'Targeted searches of French TV archives (INA, BNF) and avant-garde directors\',\n    \'total_searches\': len(search_queries),\n    \'search_queries\': search_queries,\n    \'high_relevance_candidates\': relevant_candidates,\n    \'all_search_results\': all_results,\n    \'top_candidate\': relevant_candidates[0] if relevant_candidates else None\n}\n\nfinal_file = os.path.join(\'workspace\', \'french_tv_archives_final_search.json\')\nwith open(final_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(final_search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\nprint(f"\\n=== SEARCH COMPLETE ===\\n")\nprint(f"Final results saved to: {final_file}")\n\n# Provide conclusion based on all evidence\nprint(f"\\n=== CONCLUSION ===\\n")\nprint(f"Based on comprehensive French TV archive searches:")\nprint(f"\\n1. PREVIOUS INVESTIGATION: \'Six fois deux\' by Jean-Luc Godard (1976) identified as top candidate")\nprint(f"2. ARCHIVE SEARCHES: Conducted targeted searches of INA, BNF, and director-specific queries")\nprint(f"3. METHODOLOGY: Systematic keyword analysis for all required criteria")\nprint(f"\\nMOST LIKELY ANSWER:")\nprint(f"Title: \'Six fois deux, sur et sous la communication\'")\nprint(f"Director: Jean-Luc Godard (with Anne-Marie Miéville)")\nprint(f"Year: 1976")\nprint(f"Producer: INA (Institut National de l\'Audiovisuel)")\nprint(f"\\nThis experimental television series combines:")\nprint(f"- Children\'s perspectives (episodes featuring children like \'Louison\')")\nprint(f"- Avant-garde approach (Godard\'s signature style)")\nprint(f"- Societal critique (communication and media criticism)")\nprint(f"- French TV production (INA archives)")\nprint(f"- Target era (1976 falls within 1960s-1990s range)")\nprint(f"\\nNote: Goldfish symbolism requires further episode-level investigation")',

Extract key information about top candidate\n        if \'top_candidate\' in data:\n            top_candidate = data[\'top_candidate\']\n            print(f"\\nTop candidate from previous investigation:")\n            if isinstance(top_candidate, dict) and \'candidate\' in top_candidate:\n                candidate_info = top_candidate[\'candidate\']\n                print(f"  Title: {candidate_info.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                print(f"  URL: {candidate_info.get(\'url\', \'No URL\')}")\n                print(f"  Description: {candidate_info.get(\'description\', \'No description\')[:200]}...")\n            else:\n                print(f"  Data: {str(top_candidate)[:200]}...")\n        \n        if \'confidence_assessment\' in data:\n            confidence = data[\'confidence_assessment\']\n            print(f"\\nConfidence assessment:")\n            print(f"  Match score: {confidence.get(\'match_score\', \'Unknown\')}")\n            print(f"  Confidence level: {confidence.get(\'confidence_level\', \'Unknown\')}")\n            \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"Error reading investigation file: {e}")\nelse:\n    print("\\nNo previous investigation file found")\n\nprint("\\n=== CONDUCTING FOCUSED FRENCH ARCHIVE SEARCHES ===\\n")\n\n# Define clean, focused search queries for French TV archives only\nsearch_queries = [\n    # Perform search\n        results = searcher.text(\n            query,\n            max_results=6,\n            page=1,\n            backend=["google", "duckduckgo"],\n            safesearch="off",\n            region="fr"\n        )\n        \n        if results:\n            print(f"✓ Found {len(results)} results")\n            \n            # Analyze each result\n            for j, result in enumerate(results, 1):\n                # Extract result data safely\n                title = result.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                body = result.get(\'body\', \'No body\')\n                url = result.get(\'href\', \'No URL\')\n                \n                print(f"\\n  Result {j}:")\n                print(f"    Title: {title}")\n                print(f"    URL: {url}")\n                print(f"    Body: {body[:120]}{\'...\' if len(body) > 120 else \'\'}")\n                \n                # PROPERLY DEFINE combined_text HERE before analysis\n                combined_text = f"{title} {body}".lower()\n                \n                # Define keyword categories for analysis\n                archive_keywords = [\'ina\', \'institut national audiovisuel\', \'bnf\', \'bibliothèque nationale\']\n                tv_keywords = [\'télévision\', \'television\', \'tv\', \'film tv\', \'série\']\n                children_keywords = [\'enfants\', \'enfant\', \'children\', \'child\', \'kids\', \'louison\']\n                goldfish_keywords = [\'poisson rouge\', \'goldfish\', \'poisson\', \'fish\']\n                critique_keywords = [\'critique\', \'social\', \'société\', \'societal\', \'avant-garde\']\n                director_keywords = [\'roger blin\', \'jean-marie serreau\', \'claude régy\', \'pierre chabert\', \'godard\']\n                era_keywords = [\'1960\', \'1970\', \'1980\', \'1990\', \'1976\']\n                \n                # Calculate relevance score\n                relevance_score = 0\n                relevance_score += len(archive_found) * 3    # Archive sources highly relevant\n                relevance_score += len(tv_found) * 2         # TV medium essential\n                relevance_score += len(children_found) * 4   # Children themes key\n                relevance_score += len(goldfish_found) * 4   # Goldfish symbolism key\n                relevance_score += len(critique_found) * 2   # Societal critique important\n                relevance_score += len(director_found) * 3   # Target directors important\n                relevance_score += len(era_found) * 1        # Era relevance\n                \n                # Brief delay between searches\n\nprint(f"\\n=== ANALYSIS OF SEARCH RESULTS ===\\n")\nprint(f"Total searches conducted: {len(search_queries)}")\nprint(f"Total high-relevance candidates found: {len(relevant_candidates)}")\n\nif relevant_candidates:\n    # Look for the main investigation file\n    investigation_file = None\n    for file in json_files:\n        if \'french_tv\' in file.lower() and \'investigation\' in file.lower():\n            investigation_file = file\n            break\n    \n    if investigation_file:\n        filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, investigation_file)\n        print(f"\\nInspecting: {investigation_file}")\n        \n        try:\n            with open(filepath, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                investigation_data = json.load(f)\n            \n            print("File structure:")\n            for key in investigation_data.keys():\n                print(f"  - {key}")\n            \n            # Extract key information about top candidate\n            if \'top_candidate\' in investigation_data:\n                top_candidate = investigation_data[\'top_candidate\']\n                print(f"\\nTop candidate from previous investigation:")\n                if isinstance(top_candidate, dict) and \'candidate\' in top_candidate:\n                    candidate_info = top_candidate[\'candidate\']\n                    print(f"  Title: {candidate_info.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                    print(f"  URL: {candidate_info.get(\'url\', \'No URL\')}")\n                    print(f"  Description: {candidate_info.get(\'description\', \'No description\')[:200]}...")\n                \n            if \'confidence_assessment\' in investigation_data:\n                confidence = investigation_data[\'confidence_assessment\']\n                print(f"\\nConfidence assessment:")\n                print(f"  Match score: {confidence.get(\'match_score\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                print(f"  Confidence level: {confidence.get(\'confidence_level\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error reading investigation file: {e}")\n    else:\n        print("\\nNo previous investigation file found")\nelse:\n    print("No workspace directory found")\n\nprint("\\n=== CONDUCTING CLEAN FRENCH ARCHIVE SEARCHES ===\\n")\n\n# Define clean, focused search queries for French TV archives only\nsearch_queries = [\n    # Perform search\n        results = searcher.text(\n            query,\n            max_results=6,\n            page=1,\n            backend=["google", "duckduckgo"],\n            safesearch="off",\n            region="fr"\n        )\n        \n        if results:\n            print(f"✓ Found {len(results)} results")\n            \n            # PROPERLY DEFINE text_for_analysis HERE before using it\n                text_for_analysis = f"{title} {body}".lower()\n                \n                # Define keyword categories for analysis\n                archive_keywords = [\'ina\', \'institut national audiovisuel\', \'bnf\', \'bibliothèque nationale\']\n                tv_keywords = [\'télévision\', \'television\', \'tv\', \'film tv\', \'série\']\n                children_keywords = [\'enfants\', \'enfant\', \'children\', \'child\', \'kids\', \'louison\']\n                goldfish_keywords = [\'poisson rouge\', \'goldfish\', \'poisson\', \'fish\']\n                critique_keywords = [\'critique\', \'social\', \'société\', \'societal\', \'avant-garde\']\n                director_keywords = [\'roger blin\', \'jean-marie serreau\', \'claude régy\', \'pierre chabert\', \'godard\']\n                era_keywords = [\'1960\', \'1970\', \'1980\', \'1990\', \'1976\']\n                \n                # Check for keyword matches using the properly defined variable\n                archive_found = [kw for kw in archive_keywords if kw in text_for_analysis]\n                tv_found = [kw for kw in tv_keywords if kw in text_for_analysis]\n                children_found = [kw for kw in children_keywords if kw in text_for_analysis]\n                goldfish_found = [kw for kw in goldfish_keywords if kw in text_for_analysis]\n                critique_found = [kw for kw in critique_keywords if kw in text_for_analysis]\n                director_found = [kw for kw in director_keywords if kw in text_for_analysis]\n                era_found = [kw for kw in era_keywords if kw in text_for_analysis]\n                \n                # Calculate relevance score\n                relevance_score = 0\n                relevance_score += len(archive_found) * 3    # Archive sources highly relevant\n                relevance_score += len(tv_found) * 2         # TV medium essential\n                relevance_score += len(children_found) * 4   # Children themes key\n                relevance_score += len(goldfish_found) * 4   # Goldfish symbolism key\n                relevance_score += len(critique_found) * 2   # Societal critique important\n                relevance_score += len(director_found) * 3   # Target directors important\n                relevance_score += len(era_found) * 1        # Era relevance\n                \n                # Display significant matches\n                if archive_found:\n                    print(f"    *** ARCHIVE MATCH: {archive_found} ***")\n                if tv_found:\n                    print(f"    *** TV MEDIUM: {tv_found} ***")\n                if children_found:\n                    print(f"    *** CHILDREN THEMES: {children_found} ***")\n                if goldfish_found:\n                    print(f"    *** GOLDFISH THEMES: {goldfish_found} ***")\n                if critique_found:\n                    print(f"    *** CRITIQUE THEMES: {critique_found} ***")\n                if director_found:\n                    print(f"    *** DIRECTOR MATCH: {director_found} ***")\n                if era_found:\n                    print(f"    *** ERA MATCH: {era_found} ***")\n                \n                print(f"    Relevance Score: {relevance_score}")\n                \n                #     "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom ddgs import DDGS\nimport time\n\nprint("=== FRENCH TV ARCHIVES INVESTIGATION: FINAL CLEAN SEARCH ===")\nprint("Objective: Find French TV films (1960s-1990s) with children\'s perspectives, goldfish symbolism, societal critique")\nprint("Focus: INA, BNF archives and avant-garde directors (Blin, Serreau, Régy, Chabert)\\n")\n\n# First, inspect existing investigation files to understand current findings\nprint("=== INSPECTING EXISTING INVESTIGATION FILES ===\\n")\n\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nif os.path.exists(workspace_dir):\n    json_files = [f for f in os.listdir(workspace_dir) if f.endswith(\'.json\')]\n    print(f"Found {len(json_files)} JSON files in workspace")\n    \n    # Look for the main investigation file\n    investigation_file = None\n    for file in json_files:\n        if \'french_tv\' in file.lower() and \'investigation\' in file.lower():\n            investigation_file = file\n            break\n    \n    if investigation_file:\n        filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, investigation_file)\n        print(f"\\nInspecting: {investigation_file}")\n        \n        try:\n            with open(filepath, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                investigation_data = json.load(f)\n            \n            print("File structure:")\n            for key in investigation_data.keys():\n                print(f"  - {key}")\n            \n            # Extract key information about top candidate\n            if \'top_candidate\' in investigation_data:\n                top_candidate = investigation_data[\'top_candidate\']\n                print(f"\\nTop candidate from previous investigation:")\n                if isinstance(top_candidate, dict) and \'candidate\' in top_candidate:\n                    candidate_info = top_candidate[\'candidate\']\n                    print(f"  Title: {candidate_info.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                    print(f"  URL: {candidate_info.get(\'url\', \'No URL\')}")\n                    print(f"  Description: {candidate_info.get(\'description\', \'No description\')[:200]}...")\n                \n            if \'confidence_assessment\' in investigation_data:\n                confidence = investigation_data[\'confidence_assessment\']\n                print(f"\\nConfidence assessment:")\n                print(f"  Match score: {confidence.get(\'match_score\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                print(f"  Confidence level: {confidence.get(\'confidence_level\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error reading investigation file: {e}")\n    else:\n        print("\\nNo previous investigation file found")\nelse:\n    print("No workspace directory found")\n\nprint("\\n=== CONDUCTING FOCUSED FRENCH ARCHIVE SEARCHES ===\\n")\n\n# Define clean, focused search queries for French TV archives\nsearch_queries = [\n    # Direct verification searches for the identified candidate\n    \'\\"Six fois deux\\" Godard 1976 INA television children\',\n    \'Jean-Luc Godard \\"Six fois deux\\" 1976 enfants\',\n    \n    # INA archive searches\n    \'INA \\"Institut National Audiovisuel\\" television enfants 1970s\',\n    \'INA archives télévision française enfants poisson 1960s 1970s\',\n    \n    # Perform search\n        results = searcher.text(\n            query,\n            max_results=6,\n            page=1,\n            backend=["google", "duckduckgo"],\n            safesearch="off",\n            region="fr"\n        )\n        \n        if results:\n            print(f"✓ Found {len(results)} results")\n            \n            # Analyze each result with proper variable scoping\n            for j, result in enumerate(results, 1):\n                # Extract result data safely with defaults\n                result_title = result.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                result_body = result.get(\'body\', \'No body\')\n                result_url = result.get(\'href\', \'No URL\')\n                \n                print(f"\\n  Result {j}:")\n                print(f"    Title: {result_title}")\n                print(f"    URL: {result_url}")\n                print(f"    Body: {result_body[:120]}{\'...\' if len(result_body) > 120 else \'\'}")\n                \n                # CRITICAL FIX: Define analysis_text immediately after extraction and before any analysis\n                analysis_text = f"{result_title} {result_body}".lower()\n                \n                # Define keyword categories for comprehensive analysis\n                archive_keywords = [\'ina\', \'institut national audiovisuel\', \'bnf\', \'bibliothèque nationale\']\n                tv_keywords = [\'télévision\', \'television\', \'tv\', \'film tv\', \'série\']\n                children_keywords = [\'enfants\', \'enfant\', \'children\', \'child\', \'kids\', \'louison\']\n                goldfish_keywords = [\'poisson rouge\', \'goldfish\', \'poisson\', \'fish\']\n                critique_keywords = [\'critique\', \'social\', \'société\', \'societal\', \'avant-garde\']\n                director_keywords = [\'roger blin\', \'jean-marie serreau\', \'claude régy\', \'pierre chabert\', \'godard\']\n                era_keywords = [\'1960\', \'1970\', \'1980\', \'1990\', \'1976\']\n                \n                # Check for keyword matches using the properly defined analysis_text\n                archive_matches = [kw for kw in archive_keywords if kw in analysis_text]\n                tv_matches = [kw for kw in tv_keywords if kw in analysis_text]\n                children_matches = [kw for kw in children_keywords if kw in analysis_text]\n                goldfish_matches = [kw for kw in goldfish_keywords if kw in analysis_text]\n                critique_matches = [kw for kw in critique_keywords if kw in analysis_text]\n                director_matches = [kw for kw in director_keywords if kw in analysis_text]\n                era_matches = [kw for kw in era_keywords if kw in analysis_text]\n                \n                # Calculate relevance score\n                relevance_score = 0\n                relevance_score += len(archive_matches) * 3    # Archive sources highly relevant\n                relevance_score += len(tv_matches) * 2         # TV medium essential\n                relevance_score += len(children_matches) * 4   # Children themes key\n                relevance_score += len(goldfish_matches) * 4   # Goldfish symbolism key\n                relevance_score += len(critique_matches) * 2   # Societal critique important\n                relevance_score += len(director_matches) * 3   # Target directors important\n                relevance_score += len(era_matches) * 1        # Era relevance\n                \n                # Display significant matches\n                if archive_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** ARCHIVE MATCH: {archive_matches} ***")\n                if tv_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** TV MEDIUM: {tv_matches} ***")\n                if children_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** CHILDREN THEMES: {children_matches} ***")\n                if goldfish_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** GOLDFISH THEMES: {goldfish_matches} ***")\n                if critique_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** CRITIQUE THEMES: {critique_matches} ***")\n                if director_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** DIRECTOR MATCH: {director_matches} ***")\n                if era_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** ERA MATCH: {era_matches} ***")\n                \n                print(f"    Relevance Score: {relevance_score}")\n                \n                # Store high-relevance candidates\n                if relevance_score >= 5:\n                    print(f"    *** HIGH RELEVANCE CANDIDATE ***")\n                    relevant_candidates.append({\n                        \'title\': result_title,\n                        \'url\': result_url,\n                        \'description\': result_body,\n                        \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                        \'archive_matches\': archive_matches,\n                        \'tv_matches\': tv_matches,\n                        \'children_matches\': children_matches,\n                        \'goldfish_matches\': goldfish_matches,\n                        \'critique_matches\': critique_matches,\n                        \'director_matches\': director_matches,\n                        \'era_matches\': era_matches,\n                        \'source_query\': query\n                    })\n            \n            # Store search data\n            search_data = {\n                \'query\': query,\n                \'results_count\': len(results),\n                \'results\': results\n            }\n            all_search_results.append(search_data)\n            \n        else:\n            print("✗ No results found")\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"✗ Search failed: {str(e)}")\n    \n    print("-" * 50)\n    time.sleep(1)  # Brief delay between searches\n\nprint(f"\\n=== ANALYSIS OF SEARCH RESULTS ===\\n")\nprint(f"Total searches conducted: {len(search_queries)}")\nprint(f"Total high-relevance candidates found: {len(relevant_candidates)}")\n\nif relevant_candidates:\n    # Sort by relevance score\n    relevant_candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== TOP CANDIDATES ===\\n")\n    \n    for i, candidate in enumerate(relevant_candidates[:3], 1):\n        print(f"Candidate {i} (Score: {candidate[\'relevance_score\']}):")\n        print(f"  Title: {candidate[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"  URL: {candidate[\'url\']}")\n        print(f"  Archive Matches: {candidate[\'archive_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Children Themes: {candidate[\'children_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Goldfish Themes: {candidate[\'goldfish_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Director Matches: {candidate[\'director_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Era Matches: {candidate[\'era_matches\']}")\n        print(f"  Description: {candidate[\'description\'][:150]}...")\n        print()\n    \n    # Look for the main investigation file\n    investigation_file = None\n    for file in json_files:\n        if \'french_tv\' in file.lower() and \'investigation\' in file.lower():\n            investigation_file = file\n            break\n    \n    if investigation_file:\n        filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, investigation_file)\n        print(f"\\nInspecting: {investigation_file}")\n        \n        try:\n            with open(filepath, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                investigation_data = json.load(f)\n            \n            print("File structure:")\n            for key in investigation_data.keys():\n                print(f"  - {key}")\n            \n            # Extract key information about top candidate\n            if \'top_candidate\' in investigation_data:\n                top_candidate = investigation_data[\'top_candidate\']\n                print(f"\\nTop candidate from previous investigation:")\n                if isinstance(top_candidate, dict) and \'candidate\' in top_candidate:\n                    candidate_info = top_candidate[\'candidate\']\n                    print(f"  Title: {candidate_info.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                    print(f"  URL: {candidate_info.get(\'url\', \'No URL\')}")\n                    print(f"  Description: {candidate_info.get(\'description\', \'No description\')[:200]}...")\n                \n            if \'confidence_assessment\' in investigation_data:\n                confidence = investigation_data[\'confidence_assessment\']\n                print(f"\\nConfidence assessment:")\n                print(f"  Match score: {confidence.get(\'match_score\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                print(f"  Confidence level: {confidence.get(\'confidence_level\', \'Unknown\')}")\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error reading investigation file: {e}")\n    else:\n        print("\\nNo previous investigation file found")\nelse:\n    print("No workspace directory found")\n\nprint("\\n=== CONDUCTING FOCUSED FRENCH ARCHIVE SEARCHES ===\\n")\n\n# Define clean, focused search queries for French TV archives\nsearch_queries = [\n    # Perform search\n        results = searcher.text(\n            query,\n            max_results=6,\n            page=1,\n            backend=["google", "duckduckgo"],\n            safesearch="off",\n            region="fr"\n        )\n        \n        if results:\n            print(f"✓ Found {len(results)} results")\n            \n            # Analyze each result with proper variable scoping\n            for j, result in enumerate(results, 1):\n                # Extract result data safely with defaults\n                result_title = result.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                result_body = result.get(\'body\', \'No body\')\n                result_url = result.get(\'href\', \'No URL\')\n                \n                print(f"\\n  Result {j}:")\n                print(f"    Title: {result_title}")\n                print(f"    URL: {result_url}")\n                print(f"    Body: {result_body[:120]}{\'...\' if len(result_body) > 120 else \'\'}")\n                \n                # CRITICAL FIX: Define text_analysis immediately after extraction and use consistent naming\n                text_analysis = f"{result_title} {result_body}".lower()\n                \n                # Define keyword categories for comprehensive analysis\n                archive_keywords = [\'ina\', \'institut national audiovisuel\', \'bnf\', \'bibliothèque nationale\']\n                tv_keywords = [\'télévision\', \'television\', \'tv\', \'film tv\', \'série\']\n                children_keywords = [\'enfants\', \'enfant\', \'children\', \'child\', \'kids\', \'louison\']\n                goldfish_keywords = [\'poisson rouge\', \'goldfish\', \'poisson\', \'fish\']\n                critique_keywords = [\'critique\', \'social\', \'société\', \'societal\', \'avant-garde\']\n                director_keywords = [\'roger blin\', \'jean-marie serreau\', \'claude régy\', \'pierre chabert\', \'godard\']\n                era_keywords = [\'1960\', \'1970\', \'1980\', \'1990\', \'1976\']\n                \n                # Check for keyword matches using the properly defined text_analysis variable\n                archive_matches = [kw for kw in archive_keywords if kw in text_analysis]\n                tv_matches = [kw for kw in tv_keywords if kw in text_analysis]\n                children_matches = [kw for kw in children_keywords if kw in text_analysis]\n                goldfish_matches = [kw for kw in goldfish_keywords if kw in text_analysis]\n                critique_matches = [kw for kw in critique_keywords if kw in text_analysis]\n                director_matches = [kw for kw in director_keywords if kw in text_analysis]\n                era_matches = [kw for kw in era_keywords if kw in text_analysis]\n                \n                # Calculate relevance score\n                relevance_score = 0\n                relevance_score += len(archive_matches) * 3    # Archive sources highly relevant\n                relevance_score += len(tv_matches) * 2         # TV medium essential\n                relevance_score += len(children_matches) * 4   # Children themes key\n                relevance_score += len(goldfish_matches) * 4   # Goldfish symbolism key\n                relevance_score += len(critique_matches) * 2   # Societal critique important\n                relevance_score += len(director_matches) * 3   # Target directors important\n                relevance_score += len(era_matches) * 1        # Era relevance\n                \n                # Display significant matches\n                if archive_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** ARCHIVE MATCH: {archive_matches} ***")\n                if tv_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** TV MEDIUM: {tv_matches} ***")\n                if children_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** CHILDREN THEMES: {children_matches} ***")\n                if goldfish_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** GOLDFISH THEMES: {goldfish_matches} ***")\n                if critique_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** CRITIQUE THEMES: {critique_matches} ***")\n                if director_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** DIRECTOR MATCH: {director_matches} ***")\n                if era_matches:\n                    print(f"    *** ERA MATCH: {era_matches} ***")\n                \n                print(f"    Relevance Score: {relevance_score}")\n                \n                # Store high-relevance candidates\n                if relevance_score >= 5:\n                    print(f"    *** HIGH RELEVANCE CANDIDATE ***")\n                    relevant_candidates.append({\n                        \'title\': result_title,\n                        \'url\': result_url,\n                        \'description\': result_body,\n                        \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                        \'archive_matches\': archive_matches,\n                        \'tv_matches\': tv_matches,\n                        \'children_matches\': children_matches,\n                        \'goldfish_matches\': goldfish_matches,\n                        \'critique_matches\': critique_matches,\n                        \'director_matches\': director_matches,\n                        \'era_matches\': era_matches,\n                        \'source_query\': query\n                    })\n            \n            # Direct verification searches for the identified candidate\n    \'"Six fois deux" Godard 1976 INA television children\',\n    \'Jean-Luc Godard "Six fois deux" 1976 enfants\',\n    \n    # INA archive searches\n    \'INA "Institut National Audiovisuel" television enfants 1970s\',\n    \'INA archives télévision française enfants poisson 1960s 1970s\',\n    \n    # Perform search\n        results = searcher.text(\n            query,\n            max_results=6,\n            page=1,\n            backend=["google", "duckduckgo"],\n            safesearch="off",\n            region="fr"\n        )\n        \n        if results:\n            print(f"✓ Found {len(results)} results")\n            \n            # Analyze each result with completely clean variable scoping\n            for j, result in enumerate(results, 1):\n                # Extract result data safely with defaults\n                title_text = result.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                body_text = result.get(\'body\', \'No body\')\n                url_text = result.get(\'href\', \'No URL\')\n                \n                print(f"\\n  Result {j}:")\n                print(f"    Title: {title_text}")\n                print(f"    URL: {url_text}")\n                print(f"    Body: {body_text[:120]}{\'...\' if len(body_text) > 120 else \'\'}")\n                \n                # CRITICAL: Define combined_analysis_text immediately after extraction\n                combined_analysis_text = f"{title_text} {body_text}".lower()\n                \n                # Define keyword categories for comprehensive analysis\n                archive_keywords = [\'ina\', \'institut national audiovisuel\', \'bnf\', \'bibliothèque nationale\']\n                tv_keywords = [\'télévision\', \'television\', \'tv\', \'film tv\', \'série\']\n                children_keywords = [\'enfants\', \'enfant\', \'children\', \'child\', \'kids\', \'louison\']\n                goldfish_keywords = [\'poisson rouge\', \'goldfish\', \'poisson\', \'fish\']\n                critique_keywords = [\'critique\', \'social\', \'société\', \'societal\', \'avant-garde\']\n                director_keywords = [\'roger blin\', \'jean-marie serreau\', \'claude régy\', \'pierre chabert\', \'godard\']\n                era_keywords = [\'1960\', \'1970\', \'1980\', \'1990\', \'1976\']\n                \n                # Check for keyword matches using the properly defined combined_analysis_text\n                found_archive = [kw for kw in archive_keywords if kw in combined_analysis_text]\n                found_tv = [kw for kw in tv_keywords if kw in combined_analysis_text]\n                found_children = [kw for kw in children_keywords if kw in combined_analysis_text]\n                found_goldfish = [kw for kw in goldfish_keywords if kw in combined_analysis_text]\n                found_critique = [kw for kw in critique_keywords if kw in combined_analysis_text]\n                found_director = [kw for kw in director_keywords if kw in combined_analysis_text]\n                found_era = [kw for kw in era_keywords if kw in combined_analysis_text]\n                \n                # Calculate relevance score\n                score = 0\n                score += len(found_archive) * 3    # Archive sources highly relevant\n                score += len(found_tv) * 2         # TV medium essential\n                score += len(found_children) * 4   # Children themes key\n                score += len(found_goldfish) * 4   # Goldfish symbolism key\n                score += len(found_critique) * 2   # Societal critique important\n                score += len(found_director) * 3   # Target directors important\n                score += len(found_era) * 1        # Era relevance\n                \n                # Display significant matches\n                if found_archive:\n                    print(f"    *** ARCHIVE MATCH: {found_archive} ***")\n                if found_tv:\n                    print(f"    *** TV MEDIUM: {found_tv} ***")\n                if found_children:\n                    print(f"    *** CHILDREN THEMES: {found_children} ***")\n                if found_goldfish:\n                    print(f"    *** GOLDFISH THEMES: {found_goldfish} ***")\n                if found_critique:\n                    print(f"    *** CRITIQUE THEMES: {found_critique} ***")\n                if found_director:\n                    print(f"    *** DIRECTOR MATCH: {found_director} ***")\n                if found_era:\n                    print(f"    *** ERA MATCH: {found_era} ***")\n                \n                print(f"    Relevance Score: {score}")\n                \n                # Store high-relevance candidates\n                if score >= 5:\n                    print(f"    *** HIGH RELEVANCE CANDIDATE ***")\n                    relevant_candidates.append({\n                        \'title\': title_text,\n                        \'url\': url_text,\n                        \'description\': body_text,\n                        \'relevance_score\': score,\n                        \'archive_matches\': found_archive,\n                        \'tv_matches\': found_tv,\n                        \'children_matches\': found_children,\n                        \'goldfish_matches\': found_goldfish,\n                        \'critique_matches\': found_critique,\n                        \'director_matches\': found_director,\n                        \'era_matches\': found_era,\n                        \'source_query\': query\n                    })\n            \n            # Store search data\n            search_data = {\n                \'query\': query,\n                \'results_count\': len(results),\n                \'results\': results\n            }\n            all_search_results.append(search_data)\n            \n        else:\n            print("✗ No results found")\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"✗ Search failed: {str(e)}")\n    \n    print("-" * 50)\n    time.sleep(1)  #
